<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тошный.html>то́шный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tóšnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)тошне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)тошне́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> nauseating, disgusting, sickening</li>

***тощий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тощий.html>то́щий</a> (4400)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tъščь</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*tuskjas</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*tus-sḱ-yós</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*tews-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to empty</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*tew-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to swell</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">czczy</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">tùščias</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">tukšs</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vedic_Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Vedic Sanskrit">Vedic Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">तुच्छ्य</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tucchyá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">تهی‎</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tohi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тощий.html>то́щий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tóščij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:тощий.html>тоще́е</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:тощий.html>тоще́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>gaunt, scrawny, thin</li></ol>

***трава.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:трава.html>трава́</a> (741)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*trava</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">grass</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from the PIE root <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*treh₁-</i>. Related to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дрова.html>дрова́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">drová</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">firewood</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:травить.html>трави́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">travítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to spoil or damage the grass</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тереть.html>тере́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">terétʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to rub</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τρώγω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trṓgō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I ate, devour</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трава.html>трава́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">travá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трава.html>травы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трава.html>тра́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трава.html>тра́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>grass</li>
<li>herb</li>
<li>weed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">медоно́сные <b><a href = vnd.unilang:трава.html>тра́вы</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">medonósnyje <b>trávy</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">melliferous <b>herbs</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> marijuana, weed (<i>or any other vegetative drug; also</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:травка.html>тра́вка</a>)</li></ol>

***травести.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:травести.html>травести́</a> (10063)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">travesti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:травести.html>травести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">travestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">theater<span class="ib-comma">,</span> inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> travesti role <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">theatrical role of a boy or young man, played by an actress dressed as a man</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">theater<span class="ib-comma">,</span> inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> job of an actress (or actor in rare cases) playing a travesti role
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исполнительница.html>исполни́тельница</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:травести.html>травести́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ispolnítelʹnica <b>travestí</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">female travesti performer</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">theater<span class="ib-comma">,</span> animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> travesti actress <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">an actress playing a travesti role</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a type of humorous poetry, characterized by grotesque parody or satire</li></ol>

</ol>

<ol><li>росточек</li>

***травить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:травить.html>трави́ть</a> (8724)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*traviti</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">травити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">traviti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">трави́ти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">travýty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">тра́вити</i> (first singular <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">тра̑ви̑м</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">tráviti</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">trávit᾽</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">trawić</i> (first singular <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">trawię</i>). Further cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τρώω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trṓō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hurt</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τιτρώσκω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">titrṓskō</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τρύ̄ω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trú̄ō</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">drawa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">threat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">drōа</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">threat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">þrēа</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">threat, punishment</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More distantly related to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тереть.html>тере́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">terétʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to rub</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:травить.html>трави́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">travítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to poison
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:травить.html>трави́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:крыса.html>кры́с</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:таракан.html>тарака́нов</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>travítʹ</b> krys (tarakánov)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to exterminate/destroy rats (cockroaches)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:травить.html>трави́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душу</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>travítʹ</b> dušu komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make someone feel sore at heart; disturb someone's peace of mind</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отравить.html>отрави́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otravítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to etch
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вытравить.html>вы́травить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">výtravitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(grass)</i> to trample down, to spoil, to damage
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">потрави́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">potravítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to hunt
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:травить.html>трави́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>travítʹ</b> sobákami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to set the dogs (on)</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затравить.html>затрави́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zatravítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to persecute, to badger, to torment
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затравить.html>затрави́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zatravítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pay out, to slacken out, to slack away, to ease out, to veer
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быстро.html>бы́стро</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:травить.html>трави́ть</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">býstro <b>travítʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to slack away roundly</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tell
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:травить.html>трави́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:анекдот.html>анекдо́ты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>travítʹ</b> anekdóty</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to tell jokes</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:травить.html>трави́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:байка.html>ба́йки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>travítʹ</b> bájki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to tell tall tales</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трава.html>трава́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">travá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:травка.html>тра́вка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trávka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:травка.html>тра́вки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:травка.html>тра́вки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:травка.html>тра́вок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трава.html>трава́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">travá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: grass</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> marijuana <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">or any other vegetative drug; also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трава.html>трава́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">travá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хочу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:покурить.html>покури́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:травка.html>тра́вку</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тобо́й</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja xočú pokurítʹ <b>trávku</b> s tobój.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I want to smoke <b>weed</b> with you.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> etching (<i>the process</i>)</li></ol>

<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:действие.html>де́йствие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́нию</a> гл. <a href = vnd.unilang:травить.html>трави́ть</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:преследование.html>пресле́дование</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зверь.html>зве́ря</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:птица.html>пти́цы</a>, реже — <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́ка</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:обычно.html>обы́чно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:охота.html>охо́те</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ками</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ловчий.html>ло́вчими</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:птица.html>пти́цами</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:гон.html>гон</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>

***травма.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:травма.html>тра́вма</a> (4219)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:травма.html>тра́вма</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trávma</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:травма.html>тра́вмы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:травма.html>тра́вмы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:травма.html>тра́вм</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>trauma, injury (any serious injury to the body, often resulting from violence or an accident)</li></ol>

***травмировавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:травмировавший.html>травми́ровавший</a> (20396)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:травмировать.html>травми́ровать</a> (20396)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:травма.html>тра́вма</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trávma</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:травмировать.html>травми́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">travmírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to injure</li>
<li>to traumatize (physically or psychologically)</li></ol>

***травяной.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:травяной.html>травяно́й</a> (16195)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трава.html>трава́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">travá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-яно́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-janój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:травяной.html>травяно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">travjanój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> grass; grassy

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> herbaceous</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:традиция.html>тради́ция</a> (2186)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">traditio</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:традиция.html>тради́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tradícija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:традиция.html>тради́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:традиция.html>тради́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:традиция.html>тради́ций</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:трактоваться.html>трактова́ться</a> (29131)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трактовать.html>трактова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">traktovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трактоваться.html>трактова́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">traktovátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>

<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трактовать.html>трактова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">traktovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***трактор.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:трактор.html>тра́ктор</a> (3707)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tractor</i>.
